Under the Scorching Sun, Over Two Hundred Japanese Soldiers Suffer Heatstroke 31

Drills in Pursuit Warfare at the Foot of Mount Fuji; What is the Truth About Soldiers Falling One After Another? Japanese Army Authorities Keep a Tight Lip

(Tokyo) The Japanese army is conducting drills at the foot of Mount Fuji. The Tokyo Akasaka 1st Infantry Regiment also participated. Stationed in the three villages of Tomioka, Fujioka, and Suyama, they began pursuit practice on the morning of the 2nd. The weather was exceptionally hot that day. Under the scorching sun, exposed to direct sunlight, heatstroke and sunstroke cases continued to occur in the regiment, with soldiers falling one after another, some of whom went mad. The drill authorities immediately called up local reservists, youth groups, and firefighters to carry out rescue operations. At the same time, a temporary field hospital was set up in Ohara to accommodate the patients. The army authorities issued a gag order on this matter, strictly maintaining secrecy and not discussing the truth, so it is difficult to know the news. However, it seems that no fewer than 250 people were sick, including 7 deaths and 20 seriously ill, which is a confirmed fact. (Japan United Press, 3rd)

(Tokyo) The battle line of the troops that suffered sunstroke stretched for several miles. The incident occurred just as the two armies were about to attack in skirmish formation. The army authorities immediately ordered the drills to be stopped and sent personnel to search for the sick, while seriously guarding the surrounding area. (Japan United Press, 3rd)

(Tokyo) After the tragedy at the foot of Mount Fuji, the army authorities notified Army Minister Araki, who was traveling, and held a meeting within the Army Ministry to deal with the aftermath. The responsibility for failing to establish sanitation and rescue equipment in the drill plan, which led to the loss of soldiers' lives and the illness of a large number of soldiers, naturally lies with the commanding officer. According to the observation of the army authorities, the reasons are roughly as follows: (1) Marching in scorching heat and hot wind; (2) Soldiers were exhausted from advancing in skirmish formation; (3) The troops advanced rapidly to the planned destination due to tactical reasons; (4) The terrain was sloping and had no trees to shade the sunlight. (Japan United Press, 3rd)

(Tokyo) In the drills at the foot of Mount Fuji, sunstroke suddenly occurred. The Army Ministry today issued a special announcement on the details: On the 2nd, during a joint drill by the 1st Infantry Brigade, from 11:00 AM to 2:00 PM, patients with sunstroke suddenly occurred in the 1st Regiment, including 7 deaths. The humid hot wind on that day was a southerly wind. The sunstroke patients occurred in the 1st Regiment during the encounter battle with the Kofu Regiment due to the regiment's rapid march. The 7 deaths were treated as deaths in action and were given generous awards for their merits. Among them, five second-class soldiers were promoted to first-class soldiers, one first-class soldier was promoted to corporal, and one corporal-level candidate was also promoted to corporal. (Den-tsu News Agency)

Negotiations for the Sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway Commence Substantive Discussions 35

Russian and Japanese Opinions Diverge Greatly: Japan Wants to Use the Karakhan Declaration as the Basis; Russia Insists on the 1924 Agreement

(Tokyo) The third meeting for the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway was held today, commencing substantive discussions. The core of the discussions naturally revolved around the price issue, but the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway's subsidiary businesses was also included in the discussions. The most important of these were the Chalainor coal mine, forestry, and over a dozen power plants along the line. Commercial subsidiaries include Songhua River shipping, the Harbin water and electricity lumber mill, the Harbin stadium and hotels, etc. The transfer of the export cargo wharf at Vladivostok Port will also be negotiated together. (3rd Domei News Agency Telegram)

(Tokyo) The third meeting for the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway opened at 3 PM today. It is reported that the opinions between Russia [and Manchuria] (Russia and Japan) are still greatly divergent. The content of the respective claims, which has now become clear, is as follows: (1) Russia insists on using the 1924 Sino-Soviet Agreement as the basic principle for discussing the handling of all rights and obligations of the Chinese Eastern Railway. (2) The puppet state (actually Japan) claims to use the 1919 and 1920 Karakhan Declarations as the basis, stating that Russia has abandoned the Chinese Eastern Railway as the starting point for negotiations. Therefore, the claims of the two sides are far apart. (3) The Japanese Army also claims that there is a secret agreement between China and Russia aimed at infringing upon Japan's independence, saying that Li Hongzhang of the former Qing Dynasty signed a secret agreement with Tsarist Russia in May 1896. Based on this historical fact, Japan does not need to spend a considerable price to purchase the Chinese Eastern Railway. The actual power of the Chinese Eastern Railway has fallen into the hands of the Japanese army since September 18th, and at present, Soviet Russia has no way to recover it. Japan does not need to spend huge sums of money on malicious aggressors to reward their unsuccessful ambitions, so whether or not to purchase it has little to do with Japan. (4) The Japanese military and the Foreign Ministry, based on the claims listed in item 3, have vastly different valuations of the Chinese Eastern Railway itself compared to the Russian side. The Chinese Eastern Railway also has affiliated businesses such as forestry, coal mining, transportation, insurance, finance, warehousing, customs clearance, consignment sales, wool dyeing factories, hydraulic packaging factories, and electrical businesses. Once separated from the Chinese Eastern Railway, their value is equal to zero. The Japanese side advocates for separate discussions, with the intention of seizing various Russian economic forces at the lowest price. (5) Japan regards the Russian side's hospitals, schools, and various commercial organizations as major bases for propagating communism and will include them in the list to be sealed off. Given the above conflicting situations, the content expressed by both sides at today's meeting is noteworthy. (3rd China United Press Telegram)

Details of the Prosperous Peace Steamer Massacre Case Released 48

Detailed Information Distributed by the Dalian Japanese Police Department

(Dalian) It is now known that one of the perpetrators of the Prosperous Peace massacre, a man named Daoding, was a friend of the Prosperous Peace captain, Wickmann. He used to work for Xiao's Steamboat Company in Andong, but was recently dismissed by manager Xiao John due to a grounding accident involving the Xingfu (transliterated) steamboat, which Daoding had sailed from Andong to Dalian two months ago. Daoding became unemployed and came to Dalian. The other three perpetrators, one named Dien Weistman, one named Kochi, and one named Miller, arrived in Dalian six days before Daoding. The men stayed in a hotel for about a month. Later, the three men, lacking travel expenses, pestered Daoding. Daoding moved to the Seamen's Union to avoid them. However, these three men continued to press him and conspired with him to rob the Prosperous Peace. Daoding's friend, Li Cheng, associated with bandits, and Daoding was eventually swayed. On June 4, he went to Pantong with Weistman, carrying 500 silver dollars, because Weistman had pawned a pistol at a friend's place and was going to redeem it. Daoding's guilt cannot be absolved. As for what activities Kochi and Miller were engaged in at that time, it is not yet known. Another perpetrator named Xu Le apparently joined in Tianjin. Before Daoding became involved with Xiao's Steamboat Company, he had worked for various companies. He has been in the shipping industry for thirty years. Officials from the German consulate stated that it was hard to believe that Daoding had committed such a massacre. Daoding is a Prussian who is usually polite and has received a good education and possesses philosophical ideas. After Kochi and Miller were arrested, Reuters Dalian reporters were the first to meet them. The two were hiding in the mountains, in thick grass and shrubs, and had twice gone out to buy food and water from Chinese farmers over the course of twenty-eight hours. A Japanese officer happened to be going down the mountain to the city and caught a glimpse of them, and immediately arrested the two. At this time, they were weak and exhausted, and their clothes were completely wet. They surrendered. Neither of them carried any weapons. Kochi is five feet six inches tall, with a sturdy build, a slight mustache, black hair, and a dark complexion. A Reuters reporter offered him a cigarette, which Kochi accepted and smoked calmly, despite being handcuffed. He answered all questions asked by the reporter and stated that he lived at 46 Huishan Road, Shanghai. Miller is slightly taller than Kochi and appears to be very young. He stated that he had worked for the Lulin Trading Company in Shanghai. Kochi answered the reporter's questions and said, "I have killed several Chinese people, but I don't remember how many in total." He also said, "I didn't kill Wickmann. The shooting only lasted about ten minutes. We only wanted to scare them, but they became agitated themselves, so we had to kill them." Kochi also answered questions and said, "We had been planning to rob the ship since last year. This was Daoding's idea. We thought it would definitely succeed, otherwise we would not have attempted it. Our dire situation really drove us crazy." Both said that there were six accomplices in total, one of whom remained in Tianjin. They also said that Daoding did not know Captain Wickmann. Kochi also said that they had four pistols in total, two of which were useless. He threw one into the sea before disembarking in Dalian. He confirmed that they had come to Dalian to purchase food and were going to sail the ship to Valparaiso to sell the cargo and the ship together. However, he did not initially know if there would be a buyer in that port. Kochi continued, "We didn't have time to think when we were killing people. Afterwards, it seemed quite funny, but it was too late to regret it." Before the ship hit the reef, he thought that the job had been completed. Kochi denied that any Chinese people had been imprisoned on the ship until he and his companions left the ship. After landing, he and Miller wandered in the mountains, craving cigarettes. Miller said, "We were initially overjoyed, but what's the use now? It's too late to regret it. I have parents and a sister in Germany. I don't know what they will think when they hear that I'm a thief." All the defendants are single men. Only Kochi is unemployed, and the rest are dissatisfied with their respective occupations. According to their statements, the police department treated them well. Kochi said that one of the five criminals, Xu Le, whose real name is Schroeder, was an engineer at the Shanghai Dentons Trading Company. Another man named Weistman had run a hotel, which closed down at the end of 1932, and had also been a butcher. He lived on Albert Road in Shanghai. (2nd Reuters Telegram)

(Dalian) The police department released details of the Prosperous Peace ship massacre this afternoon, stating that the Prosperous Peace ship loaded 1,800 tons of coal on June 26 before sailing from Dagu to Fuzhou. The German Daoding and his accomplices Müller and four others requested to board the ship as passengers and were granted permission by the captain of the Prosperous Peace. When the ship reached about two hundred miles northeast of Shanghai, the five criminals attacked the crew with guns, killing the Russian captain and his wife, a Russian engineer, a Chinese radio operator, and six Chinese sailors. Their bodies were thrown into the sea. Other details are the same as reported in the previous telegram. (3rd Reuters Telegram)

(Dalian) Weistman, one of the perpetrators of the Prosperous Peace massacre, is tall and burly, and his hair has been dyed black. Kochi is a fugitive from Shanghai who was imprisoned in Shanghai for two years. Daoding was captured during the Qingdao campaign in the European War. Miller is from Elberfeld, but Schroeder's nationality is still unknown. (3rd Reuters Telegram)

Six Eastern European Countries Sign Security Pact 86

Reuters dispatch from London on the 3rd: The Russian delegation announced tonight that the Soviet Union, Romania, Turkey, Poland, Estonia, and Latvia have signed a non-aggression pact based on the definition of aggression proposed by the Soviet Foreign Minister at the Geneva Disarmament Conference on May 23rd. It is reported that Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov and Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu signed a Russian-Romanian treaty on Saturday night as a precursor to today's signing of a regional multilateral security pact. The pact implies the resolution of the 14-year-long Bessarabian dispute between the two countries, and it is agreed that Moscow and the Little Entente countries will soon fully restore diplomatic relations. As for the non-aggression pact between the Soviet Union and the Little Entente countries, it is reported that it will be signed on Tuesday, after which Litvinov will go to Europe for a rest, viewing it as a great accomplishment, and he has nothing else to linger for.

Havas dispatch from Paris on the 2nd: The definition of an aggressor was initially proposed by the Soviet representative at the Disarmament Conference, and later Greek representative Politis submitted a draft in the Security Council, which was mostly approved by various countries. Recently, representatives from the Soviet Union, Poland, and the Little Entente countries held negotiations outside of the economic conference, establishing a pact to accept the definition proposed by Politis. Last night, representatives from the Soviet Union, Poland, Turkey, some Little Entente countries, and the Baltic states signed the agreement. France has recently issued a semi-official statement saying that this agreement is a major guarantee for peace in Eastern Europe.

French Newspaper Reports on Germany's New Military Organization 87

Organization Possesses Combat Capability; Hitler Claims It is Not an Army but a Police Force

Havas dispatch from Paris on the 2nd: This newspaper, Qing Yi Bao, discusses German military preparations, stating that [the National Socialist Party's military organization has been completed. Its detailed organization is known externally. The smallest unit of the National Socialist Party's army is called Sharc, with 20 soldiers commanded by a junior officer, equivalent to a platoon in a regular army. Five Schaarcs combine into a Trupp, equivalent to a company under a first lieutenant in a regular army. Four or five Trupps combine into a Starn, equivalent to a battalion in a regular army. Above that is the StarnBanp, about 1,500 men, equivalent to a regiment in a regular army. The strongest unit of the army is the brigade, which, in addition to regiments, also has other special units, namely: (1) six motorcycle and bicycle squads for reconnaissance and ensuring the safety of the army, equivalent to the old cavalry; (2) 14 bombers skilled in bombing; (3) three engineer squads, each with three connecting links, with motorboats and machine guns, so they are rich in attack capability. Recently, an engineer company has conducted joint exercises with the Steel Helmet Party and the police several times. German Chancellor Hitler said that the groups organized by the Nazi Party are only for domestic police use and have nothing to do with the army. This statement does not match the facts. In reality, Germany's military preparations are extremely strong and prepared for combat. Those who advocate that France should disarm are either criminals or the greatest fools in the world.]

Japanese Military-Police Conflict Case 89

In the future, if there is any such improper police behavior that damages the prestige of the Imperial Army and damages the reputation of soldiers, in order to protect soldiers, it may be necessary to take necessary measures." Outline of Japan's New Diplomatic Path 91

Conspiring to Contact Our Provinces, Attempting to Undermine Unification

Forcing Us to Sign Political, Economic, and Military Alliance with Military Force

Forcing Us to Hand Over National Defense and Security Rights to Japanese Military

Tokyo Correspondence, June 28: The Tokyo Yomiuri Shimbun published the Japanese government's new diplomatic principles in large headline characters. Its content is not far from the news reported by the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun, but it is more detailed and concrete, expressing the content of its policy of dividing China and wanting to pursue its continental policy with military force. The original text is excerpted below for the reference of the people of the country.

[The diplomatic policy of the Imperial government after withdrawing from the League of Nations, in addition to signing peace treaties with various countries individually, will still gladly participate in international conferences and adopt cooperation with Europe and the United States as its keynote. Recently, in view of the British government's boycotting of Japanese goods, the US government's plan to expand the navy and build large warships, the world economy conference's lack of restraint, and the disarmament conference's inability, the heads of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs deeply know that it was a mistake to focus on conferences centered on Europe and the United States in the past and on diplomacy and international cooperationism. It is necessary to take advantage of the autumn when Europe and the United States are unable to take care of themselves to maintain the right of self-existence of the Far Eastern nations. Based on the principle of the three countries of China, Japan, and Manchuria adopting each other's strengths and supplementing each other's weaknesses, an alliance of the three countries in political, economic, and military affairs is created to prepare for the subsequent invasion of the white races of Europe and the United States. Adopting this principle is a prerequisite, renewing its diplomacy, so that the Empire's diplomacy returns to Asia and pays attention to the permanent solution of the Far Eastern problem. According to this claim, the Asian Division of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has ordered the various agencies stationed in China to contact the central government and local governments of China separately to inquire about their opinions. It abandons the previous diplomacy of direct negotiations with the central government and adopts a diplomatic policy of separate contacts with local areas. To the central government, it contacts Chiang Kai-shek; to the Southwest, it contacts Chen Jitang and Hu Hanmin; to Fujian, it contacts Jiang Guangding; to Hunan, it contacts He Jian; to Hubei, it contacts Xia Douyin; to Shandong, it contacts Han Fuqu; to Beiping, it contacts Huang Fu, etc., and starts direct negotiations separately. The above-mentioned alliances are signed individually with the various local governments, and a standing committee is created to handle all outstanding unresolved issues. It is heard that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has ordered Consul General Hinoh to the Nanjing government, Consul General Nishita to the Shandong Provincial government, Consul General Moriya to the Fujian Provincial government, Consul General Yoshida to the Guangdong Provincial government, Consul General Osaki to the Hubei Provincial government, and Secretary Nakayama to the Beiping Political Committee, etc., to secretly contact. If the various local governments of China agree, formal negotiations may begin in September, and Minister Arima will be ordered to return to the country to contact the negotiating methods.]

Outline of Japan's new Far Eastern diplomatic policy: (1) The Imperial government is still willing to cooperate with Britain and the United States to the extent possible, but in order to ensure the survival rights of the Far Eastern nations, it must wait for the combination of ethnic groups of the same race and the same culture with coexistence and co-prosperity as the basis. In order to achieve its purpose, China's participation is an indispensable condition. China must stand on a proper assessment of the current situation and participate in the political, economic, and military alliance advocated by Japan. (2) In order to achieve the above-mentioned purpose, the Imperial government wants to change the previous diplomatic policy towards China, which centered on the central government. With reference to China's actual situation, it will cooperate with local governments individually. Standing on the principle of coexistence and co-prosperity, if necessary, it will provide spiritual and material assistance. Further, it will sign an alliance of offense and defense with local governments, like the Japan-Manchukuo Protocol, and Japan's imperial army will take over China's national defense and maintain China's security, especially the work of suppressing the communist bandits. (3) The above-mentioned policy adopted by the Imperial government does not contain any anti-foreign nature, but the internal forces of China, or the forces of a third country, whether expressed in the form of politics, economy, or ideology, that hinder Japan's policy, the Imperial government will resolutely use military force to eliminate and carry out its original national policy. (4) Various outstanding issues that hinder Sino-Japanese cooperation, such as China's anti-Japanese resistance to goods, the Sino-Japanese Treaty of Commerce, tariff issues, the Nishihara Loans, the suppression of the communists, extraterritorial rights, the recovery of concessions, the Shandong land issue, the opening of important cities as commercial ports, etc., are connected according to their nature either with the central government or with local areas, and a standing committee will be created to solve everything. (5) For local governments with difficult local finances, a credit system for the import of Japanese goods is created with them, and Japan has preparations to respond to their loans. Moreover, in order to form China and Japan into a large economic group, Japan wants to use Japanese cotton yarn, groceries, machinery, seafood, wheat flour, etc., to exchange for China's Daye iron, Shanxi coal, and South China raw cotton, etc. China and Japan adopt each other's strengths and make up for each other's weaknesses to revive the economy of the Far East.

Whereabouts of Three Warships Unknown 92

Moving Further Away From Qingdao; Seemingly Heading South

Jinan Correspondence: The naval mutiny in Qingdao has a considerable relationship with the security of the Shandong coast. Provincial Chairman Han Fuqu sent Provincial Committee member Zhang Yue to Qingdao to comfort Mr. Shen and mediate the return of the three naval vessels. Shen did not add any blame. Now the three warships seem to have sailed to Guangdong, and it is not easy to recover them. The coastal security in the future must be planned separately. Shen Honglie originally planned to come to Jinan with Ge Guangting to visit Han and discuss, but because the people of Qingdao had just calmed down, it was inconvenient to leave, so he asked Ge to represent him and come to Jinan to visit Han and report and discuss everything. Ge arrived in Jinan with Qing at 7:40 this morning (the 2nd). Han's representative Zhang Yue also came with him. Han, the Director of the Industry Department Wang Fangting, the Mayor of Jinan Kai Chenglie, and the former Commander-in-Chief of the Fifth Route Army Wang Jinyu, etc., all went to the station to welcome him. After Ge got off the train, he went to the Jiaoji Hotel with Han and the welcomers to rest. The reporter visited and asked about the details of the three warships. Ge answered one by one and recorded them as follows.

Three Ships Sailing South 93

Ge stated, "When the three ships first sailed away, they often communicated with Commander Shen by radio, asking Shen to step down. Shen had already agreed. There has been no news in the past three days. Qingdao sent radio messages, but they did not respond. However, according to the length of the radio waves they transmitted before, the three ships are getting farther and farther away from Qingdao and seem to be heading south, and are thousands of miles away from our country's coast. There are many merchant ships traveling between Qingdao, Dalian, and Shanghai, but no trace of these ships has been seen, because they are afraid of being pursued, so they are far away from the coast. As for the reason for sailing to Guangdong, it is because of the previous Laoshan incident. The person who took the initiative to harm Shen was a Cantonese captain Fang, who is now the commander of a Cantonese fort. Fang was the former education chief of the Huludao Naval Academy. The perpetrators this time were all Huludao students and had a considerable relationship with Fang. The three ships have enough coal to use, and although there is not much fresh water, they can barely use seawater to relieve the emergency.

Shen's Attitude 94

After the incident, Mayor Shen immediately telegraphed the central government to resign from all his positions. The central government sent a telegram of comfort and retention. Chairman Han also sent Committee Member Zhang (Yue) to comfort and retain him. I once advised Mr. Shen with Committee Member Zhang not to resign. Shen said that now, in order to be responsible to the end, he would never rush to leave again, because although the three ships have left, many of their family members are still in Qingdao. They are actually colleagues in distress for more than ten years. Now, although they have betrayed me, I will never betray them. I will definitely arrange for their family members properly, and the Qingdao municipal administration must also be handled, so as long as I am in office for one day, I will be responsible for one day. Qingdao is now as calm as ever. The consuls of various countries and the naval commanders of various countries were all surprised by this incident, and expressed their sympathy to Mayor Shen. It is not difficult to chase back the three ships, but Mayor Shen is taking into account the dignity of the country and is unwilling to do this. My visit to Jinan this time is to report to Chairman Han on behalf of Mayor Shen and contact everything. It will take three or two days before I can return to Qingdao."

The True Cause of the Incident 95

The reasons for this incident have been published in various reports, but they are nothing more than the Laoshan incident last year. Those who saved Shen asked for excessive rewards, and Shen was unwilling to use the country's salary to make personal entertainment, so they harbored resentment. For example, Feng Zhichong, who stabbed Shen, was only a junior officer at the time, and afterwards asked to be the director of the port administration and the transportation office and the captain of the security brigade, but Shen did not approve them. In less than a year, he was promoted to senior officer, but was still dissatisfied. Guan, who worked the hardest to save Shen, was given 8,000 yuan by Shen afterwards, but he was also dissatisfied. The conspiracy to overthrow Shen was not a one-day affair. Although there was no background in advance this time, there was definitely a plan, which can be proved by the simultaneous departure of the three ships. However, Ling Xiao, who plotted to harm Shen the year before last, is now in Beiping and does not seem to have heard about this matter.

Han Fuqu Speaks 96

I originally intended to mediate in the middle so that the three ships could return, and Mayor Shen would not add any blame to them. Now that they have gone far and have not seen a reply, Mayor Shen has also not sent a reply. All the details are not very clear. After Committee Chairman Ge (Guangting) came to Jinan, I heard the details. However, I advised Shen not to resign as mayor, and Shen has indicated that he will no longer insist on resigning. (2nd)

Guizhou Representative in Guangdong Talks About Military Affairs and Transportation; Hunan Plane Suddenly Flees to Guizhou

The civil aviation between Guizhou and Guilin is being planned to facilitate transportation and transmission. In addition, it is reported that a negotiation incident has recently occurred between Guizhou and Hunan. The reason is that in mid-June, Hunan's He Jian ordered the Changsha Aviation Office to send a plane to the border area for reconnaissance because Xiangxi in Hunan Province was bordering Guizhou Province and the two factions of Wang and Liu in Guizhou Province were fighting and stray soldiers and bandits often ran into Xiangxi. Huang Fei, the director of the aviation office, ordered Deputy Captain Zhou Yiping to drive a single-wing plane called "Lange" to conduct reconnaissance in the Xiangxi area. The plane went missing after that. The Hunan authorities telegraphed various parties to inquire. It was not until mid-June that they received a report that the plane Lange had fled to Guizhou Province and the pilot had been appointed as the captain of the Guizhou Aviation Team, etc. Another rumor is that the plane fled to Guizhou due to a large sum of money. Now He Jian has filed a serious negotiation, and it is unknown how it will end. (June 28)

Looking at the entire Sichuan situation, it is all in the midst of war. Qianwei, Jiajiang, Renshou, and Jingyan are again the battlegrounds for the two Liu's competition. (July 1)

House Tax on Roads Crossing North Sichuan Road to be Collected According to Regulations 113

Public Security and Finance Bureaus Issue Joint Announcement

According to a person in charge of the Finance Bureau yesterday, the case of house tax on roads crossing North Sichuan Road has been instructed by the Municipal Government to continue to be collected according to regulations. The Public Security Bureau is currently being notified and members are being assigned to collect. The report in yesterday's newspaper, which stated that the Finance Bureau and other bureaus exchanged opinions and contacted the relevant parties separately, is not true. The joint announcement of the Public Security and Finance Bureaus is recorded as follows: Announcement of the Joint Announcement: It is hereby announced that the Municipal Government's Order No. 6030 states, "It is hereby ordered that the Municipal Government's 240th Municipal Affairs Meeting has resolved that the house tax in the area of North Sichuan Road and Laobazi Road should still be persuaded to be paid. Those who incite or abet resistance to taxation should be dealt with according to law," which is on file. In addition to ordering the Public Security Bureau, it is hereby recorded and ordered that the bureau immediately comply with and handle it properly. Upon receipt of this order, it was found that the citizens in the North Sichuan Road area have made many requests for the house tax that should be paid, hoping to be spared. There is still some misunderstanding of this case. It must be known that the house tax is the cost of municipal construction and is the common obligation of all citizens. The area of North Sichuan Road has long been subject to police power, and public facilities such as water and electricity can also be supplied by the urban area. The citizens in that area have enjoyed the benefits of municipal facilities for many years and have never fulfilled their obligation to pay taxes. In other words, the citizens in the south city, Zhabei, and other districts of this city indirectly bear the burden. It is unreasonable to say that it is fair. The Finance Bureau of this city is in charge of taxes and fees, and is impartial. The purpose of opening up the house tax in that area this time is to equalize the burden on citizens and indirectly protect the interests of the majority of citizens. It is necessary to start collecting taxes on a regular basis. The citizens in that area should actively comply with and pay taxes to show fairness. If they claim that the commerce is depressed after the war and do not pay the house tax, then the spring and summer house taxes in the war zone of this city in the 21st year were exempted by the Municipal Government in June of the previous year. This has now become a past fact, and this reason cannot be established. As for the statement that the area is an extraterritorial road construction and must be paid after the extraterritorial road problem is resolved, it is even more unreasonable. The citizens who live in the extraterritorial road construction area, because the municipal public facilities have not yet reached, and are now using the water and electricity of the special zone, and paying the house tax of the special zone, this city is temporarily no longer collecting taxes in order to relieve the difficulties of the people, so as to avoid the burden of repetition. Now that the facts are different, it is not appropriate to discuss them together. There must be no shortage of citizens who are well aware of the truth and can understand this purpose. The aforementioned reasons for the order have been issued by the Finance Bureau to the Municipal Tax Collection Office to collect taxes according to regulations, and the Public Security Bureau has ordered the district offices in charge to assist in the handling. We are sincerely afraid that someone will incite and obstruct the collection of taxes. Therefore, we have jointly issued an announcement, urging the citizens to embrace the concept of municipal administration and pay the house tax as soon as possible, and not to lightly believe in rumors and delay any further. We have high hopes for the bureaus, etc. This announcement.

Yu Hongjun and Fei Dun Continued to Discuss Factory Inspection Yesterday 114

Discussion on One Part of the Three Key Points Fei Xindun's Talk Shows Slight Progress It is reported that the Department of Industry and the Municipal Government have completed the discussion on the method of factory inspection in the Public Concession. Yu Hongjun, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, visited Fei Xindun, Director of the Public Works Bureau, yesterday afternoon. The details are as follows:

Key Points of the Method 115

The key points of the method discussed by Secretary-General Yu and Director Fei were announced yesterday by the Labor Department of the Ministry of Industry in Beijing, namely ㈠ The two parties form a committee with seven members, four from our side and three from the Public Works Bureau. The chairman belongs to us, the vice-chairman belongs to them, and the salaries of the staff are borne equally. ㈡ Chinese labor laws can be implemented in the concession. ㈢ Regarding violations of Chinese labor laws, the power to prosecute and punish is exercised by the Chinese local court. When the reporter asked Mr. Yu about the above three key points yesterday, he did not deny them, but thought that it was too early to publish them before they were resolved.

Yu Visits Fei 116

After the method was drafted, the Municipal Government consulted the Ministry of Industry for opinions and made two revisions. Now it has been agreed, so Secretary-General Yu personally visited Director Fei Xindun of the Public Works Bureau at 3 p.m. yesterday. Fei Xindun's Talk 117

Fei expressed his opinion that it was too early to publish the key points of the method to the Beijing News. The reporter then asked whether the meeting today was about the key points of the method in the Beijing News. Fei replied that the discussion between Secretary-General Yu and I was only part of it, not a complete discussion, because this matter still requires several discussions. Finally, the reporter asked whether a date for another meeting had been scheduled. He replied that Yu and I often visited each other, so the date of the next meeting has not been set.

Labor Unrest Occurred Among Workers at Shanghai Electric Power Company New Plant Yesterday 118

A worker in the furnace room fell to his death, and fellow workers in the same factory requested compensation on his behalf. As a result of mediation, work was resumed this morning. Workers at the new plant of the Shanghai Electric Power Company in the Yangshupu Public Concession have been unable to resolve the issue of compensation for workers who died on duty for a long time.

After the county refused to give a definite answer, it was proposed to each other yesterday afternoon.

First Letter from the Public Works Bureau Ordering the Yi Yuan Rubber Factory to Stop Operations 119

The reason given was that the factory building was not properly constructed. The union decided to petition the Party organs this morning.

The Yi Yuan Rubber Factory on North Chengdu Road in this port was ordered to move by the Public Works Bureau because the Public Works Bureau considered that the factory building was not suitable for manufacturing rubber. After reluctantly announcing the suspension of operations the day before yesterday, the workers were panicked. The union held a meeting yesterday to discuss and decided to petition the party and government organs this morning. The details are recorded as follows:

Letter from the Public Works Bureau 120

The Public Works Bureau of the Public Concession notified the factory to move the building, saying, "Respectfully, the acting director of the Fire Department of this bureau once stated that the building of the Yi Yuan Rubber and Leather Manufacturing Factory at No. 1002 North Chengdu Road is completely unsuitable for manufacturing rubber products and that the factory should be moved to a more suitable building, etc. In the three letters to your company on May 11, 18, and 19 of this year, you were warned. Now, I am writing to inform you again that the dangerous nature of the materials used in your factory, the conditions under which work is carried out, and the improper construction of the factory building are all sufficient to endanger life and property. If there is no sufficient and satisfactory safety guarantee for this dangerous operation, this bureau will not allow it to continue. If you do not believe that the building is sufficient for all current uses within three weeks, the bureau will file a lawsuit and exercise all its powers to prevent public danger."

Announcement of Closure 121

After receiving the notice from the Public Works Bureau, the factory announced the closure of the factory on the 29th of last month. The original text reads, "Publicly, the factory has been notified by the Public Works Bureau of the Public Concession that the structure of the factory building is not in compliance with the requirements and is limited to moving the factory within three weeks. The factory has repeatedly sent personnel to negotiate, but without success. It has now been decided to suspend operations from July 1. All workers are requested to register with the manager's office, fill in their addresses, and wait for the factory to find a new site and resume operations before notifying them to return to work. Those who voluntarily do not return to the factory or find another job midway are also free to do so. However, due to the forced suspension of operations, relocation, and site search by this factory, the losses will be huge, and the suspension of operations of the workers is deeply regrettable. However, there is nothing that can be done, except to wait for the establishment of a new factory before notifying them. This announcement."

Union Mediation 122

After receiving the news, the workers opposed the factory's closure because the factory still had a four-year lease contract for the building, and reported it to the Third District Rubber Union for mediation. The union sent Xu Yongjia, Chen Zhikang, Liang Yongyi, and others to the factory for mediation at 1 p.m. yesterday, but the manager, Huang Yongqin, was out, resulting in no results.

Petition Today 123

The union considered the situation to be serious and held an emergency meeting at the Da Wang Temple at 1:20 p.m. yesterday. More than 230 members attended, chaired by Chen Zhikang. After the chairman reported on the situation, the discussion began. It was decided ㈠ How should the sudden announcement of the factory closure affect the livelihood of the workers? It was decided (A) to submit a report to the Party and government for relief (B) and to schedule a petition to the Party and government by all on the 4th. ㈡ Should representatives be appointed to be responsible for the negotiation? It was decided to appoint Chen Zhikang, He Jinyu, Li Jiafu, Li Zanqian, Gao Huizhen, Shen Yiyun, Shen Zhukang, Yao Shouren, Wang Rensheng, Wu Jinfu, Hu Qiaodi, Shen Agen, Wu Meirong, and other 13 people to handle the matter together with the union. ㈢ How should the Public Works Bureau's unauthorized order to close the Yi Yuan Factory, which resulted in the loss of livelihood of all workers, be dealt with? It was decided (secret) ㈣ Should workers register after the factory closes in order to compile statistics? It was decided to hand it over to the Organization Department to start registration and to petition the Municipal Government, the Municipal Party Department, and the Social Affairs Bureau at 9 a.m. today.

After the implementation of the work slowdown, the detective house mediated and agreed to work as usual from today, and the factory and workers formally consulted on the 5th of this month, and the strike was resolved. The details are as follows:

Worker Dies 124

At about 2:40 p.m. on the 25th of last month, a worker in the third furnace room of the factory, a local man named Zhou (name unknown), 25 years old, was working next to a 20-foot-high furnace on that day. Several other workers were sending iron plates past him. Zhou saw that the place was narrow, so he rested against a decayed piece of bamboo, which broke, and Zhou fell down with it. His head hit a nail, which penetrated deep inside, and blood flowed like a stream. Although the factory's resident doctor tried to save him, it was ineffective, and he died on the spot.

Request for Compensation 125

After the incident, the workers believed that Zhou's death was due to work-related causes and asked the factory to provide generous compensation and allocate 2,000 yuan in compensation. The factory agreed to consider it. Recently, the representatives of the workers learned that the factory only agreed to provide 200 yuan in compensation, and believed that the factory was intentionally disregarding human life. Therefore, from 1 p.m. yesterday, more than 800 people from the copper workshop, electrical workshop, furnace room, workshop, and all the department chiefs and day laborers, all went on strike to promote the company's awareness. However, in order to maintain the traffic of current, about 400 workers of the three shifts in each workshop and department still worked as usual to avoid affecting the local area.

Police Prepared 126

At the same time, the workers sent representatives to negotiate with the factory, but the factory manager, Mr. Hoppergen, had returned to the United States, and the acting factory manager, Haierte, also said that he could not answer immediately. Therefore, the workers insisted. The incident was learned by the nearby Lan Road Police Station, which believed that the work slowdown was serious, and sent a large number of Chinese and Western detectives and special police cars to guard the area. Fortunately, the striking workers strictly maintained order, so no incidents occurred. The special police also advised the workers to mediate.

By 5 p.m., it was time to leave work as usual, but the striking workers

Did not want to leave the factory.

Resume Work This Morning 127

By 5:30 p.m., the acting factory manager, Haierte, agreed to the workers' request to reply on the 5th (Wednesday) and ordered the election of two foremen representatives and three worker representatives to negotiate with the factory manager. The special police informed all the workers of the above method, who were satisfied and stopped the slowdown. However, at that time, it was time to leave work, and all the workers left the factory as usual, deciding to work as usual from today.

Elected Representatives 128

All the workers on the spot elected five representatives to wait for the factory manager's reply on the 5th: Wang Xingen, Yang Shaogen, Chen Baogen, Ni Wenfu, and Shang Shi, and decided to strictly maintain order and wait for the reply.

Real Estate Association Writes to Public Works Bureau Requesting No High Land Value Assessment 129

Xin Sheng News Agency reported that the Real Estate Association of this city received a letter from Dun Yu Real Estate Company and other members yesterday, reporting that the Donation Office of the Public Works Bureau recently sent people to arbitrarily overestimate land values in the eastern district by more than 60% in order to increase tax revenue and oppress property owners by all means. Therefore, they sent a letter to the association, requesting it to protest to the Public Works Bureau and quickly stop the high land value assessment behavior to reduce the burden and relieve commercial difficulties. Therefore, the association immediately wrote to the Public Works Bureau, stating: "Since the Shanghai Incident of January 28, the commercial depression and the people's livelihood in the eastern district have been exhausted. At a time when the world economy is declining, this city is also affected. Although the houses in the district are dense, the empty houses account for three or four tenths. If this continues, the property owners themselves will find it difficult to maintain. Moreover, the problem of tap water has increased due to the high valuation of rent, which has been delayed and cannot be resolved. If the land value is overestimated, the donation amount and water price will increase at the same time, which will inevitably lead to disputes between citizens and property owners, which is a major hidden danger in society. Therefore, we sincerely request that the proposal to overestimate land values this time be canceled to relieve commercial difficulties."

Su Bingwen Talks About Planning to Settle His Subordinates 130

Decided to Send People to Investigate First and Then Ask for Relief

General Su Bingwen, accompanied by Fan Ruizheng, representative stationed in Beiping, Wang Erlu, commander of the Hulunbuir garrison, Gai Xingya, secretary, Wu Delin, brigade commander, and an adjutant, arrived in Shanghai from Hangzhou by car at about 4 p.m. the day before yesterday. The Central News Agency reporter visited General Su at his residence yesterday morning and made the following remarks:

Mission This Time 131

According to General Su, this time he went to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to report on the anti-Japanese war. The issue of settling his subordinates has not yet been discussed. The families of the generals and those compatriots who are unwilling to be slaves to a conquered country, who returned from Russia, are scattered in Xinjiang, Beiping, Shanghai, and other places, displaced and homeless. When I think of the fact that the anti-Japanese war has not yet succeeded and the territory is still in the hands of the enemy, and that my comrades have suffered such a catastrophe, I feel uneasy and distressed. Therefore, I came to Shanghai to plan a settlement plan. However, this matter is a major one and it is not easy to solve. It still needs to be considered in the long term. Now it has been decided to send people to Xinjiang, Beiping, and other places to investigate the number of people and then request the central government to provide relief.

Observation of Bandit Suppression 132

When I went to Jiangxi to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, the bandit suppression military situation was extremely tense. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek held meetings to suppress bandits for eight or nine hours a day, which was too hard, resulting in slight discomfort. The bandits in Jiangxi Province should not be underestimated. The bandit suppression army is about 200,000 people, and the work is progressing smoothly. The failure of the anti-Japanese military affairs in North China this time and the disturbances in the rear by the Jiangxi bandits were a major reason. If there were no communist bandits jumping beams internally, at least 100,000 troops could be drawn north to resist Japan, and the anti-Japanese military affairs would not have failed. From this, we can know the importance of the bandit suppression military affairs. Domestic security is the beginning of external resistance. The bandit suppression is actually the same goal by different routes and there is no distinction.

Request for Punishment 133

I am a soldier and have the duty to defend the territory. Last year, I fought bitterly in the Manchukuo and Heilongjiang area for several months, but I was unable to protect the national territory, resulting in my exile overseas. This time, I returned to the country and went to Nanjing to plead guilty to the central government and request punishment. I was deeply ashamed that the central government remembered the spirit of resistance against Japan in the past, did not add punishment, and still appointed me as a member of the Military Commission. When I was in Lushan, I received a telegram from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek informing me that the Central Political Committee had elected Chairman Ma and me as members of the Military Commission. We have telegraphed to thank you, and the official order has not yet been received.

No Intention to Go to Xinjiang 134

When my troops returned to the country from Russia via Xinjiang, there was a riot in Xinjiang Province. The capital of Xinjiang issued a small number of firearms and instructed the subordinates to stay in Xinjiang to maintain order and protect the country and defend the people. It was the duty of a soldier, so the troops stayed in Xinjiang for several months to maintain law and order, which has been highly praised by the authorities and the people. When I met Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in Nanchang, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek asked me whether I would like to go to Xinjiang to inspect my subordinates. However, I have recently been suffering from a cold and feel very uncomfortable, so I have no intention of going to Xinjiang so far.

Personal Position 135

I have always held a determination to sacrifice myself. Death is not a pity, and I have no further hopes. Therefore, I have no prejudice or desire regarding my personal fate. As long as it benefits the country and the nation, I will not hesitate to go through fire and water. I am a soldier, and my future actions will follow the orders and commands of the government.

Future Hopes 136

At this time of national crisis, the 30 million people of the Northeast are still suffering in dire straits. The land of the four provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe is still under the iron hooves of the enemy. The people of the country should quickly awaken, unite sincerely, and work together to resist foreign aggression. With years of hard work, it is hoped that we can recover the lost territories.

Meeting with Ma and Zhang 137

After General Su arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday, he went to meet with General Ma Zhanshan that evening to discuss the placement of his subordinates. Yesterday morning around 11:00 AM, he received General Zhang Dianjiu and many of his subordinates at his residence. It is expected that he will stay in Shanghai for several days.

The United Reserve of Banking Industry Will Issue New Public Notes Starting Today 151

Promoting the convenience of commerce and advocating the bill discount system

According to the New Voice News Agency, the United Reserve Committee public notes of the Shanghai Banking Association will be issued by the committee's member banks with signatures and paid by the committee. It has been a year since the issuance. Recently, in order to increase convenience, the committee's member banks have unanimously resolved to revise the format of the public notes and the public note regulations separately, and they will be issued starting today. The advantages of this new public note are: (1) The old public note was limited to immediate payment, and its use was only convenient among financial institutions. The new public note can be opened for forward delivery and can adapt to the needs of commerce. The original was a check style, but now it is a draft style. (2) The amount of the old public note was a fixed whole number. The new public note has a limited amount per sheet, and the bank can freely fill it within the limit, similar to a traveler's check. (3) The old public note only had Chinese characters. The new public note is in both Chinese and English. Shanghai is an international commercial port, and the commercial relationship between China and foreign countries is very close. Now, including English, it can circulate more smoothly. (4) In addition to retaining the original interbank lending system, the new public note can be discounted by the holder to the committee before it expires. The forward payment can be changed to cash immediately. It is not only a solid guarantee, but also a lively nature, which can be adjusted in commerce. (5) The discounting of commercial paper has been advocated by the Chinese banking industry for many years, but it has not yet developed. The discounting of public notes is handled by the committee, which is no different from the banks handling it themselves. It can be a pioneer in the discounting of commercial paper. The reporter from the New Voice News Agency specifically visited Zhu Boquan, the manager of the committee, yesterday. According to him, the lending rate on July 4 was 1.4 cents per 1,000 yuan per day, and the discount rate was 1.2 cents per 1,000 yuan per day. Both have been predetermined and will be posted daily. He received a sample of the new public note, which is well-printed and comprehensive in form. We will quickly make a plate and publish it below, along with the full text of the revised public note regulations.

Shanghai Banking Association United Reserve Committee Public Note Regulations (Revised on May 25, 1933) Article 1: The member banks of the Shanghai Banking Association United Reserve Committee (hereinafter referred to as the "member banks") shall, in accordance with the provisions of the covenant, take the property deposited with the Shanghai Banking Association United Reserve Committee (hereinafter referred to as the "committee") as the standard to receive public notes from the committee and may issue public notes. Article 2: The issuance and circulation of the public note shall record the following items and be signed by the issuing bank: (1) a fixed amount; (2) the name of the payee or business; (3) an unconditional payment commission; (4) the date of issuance; (5) the due date. If the payee is not recorded, the holder shall be the payee. If the due date is not recorded, it shall be deemed to be payable upon sight. Article 3: The amount stated on the public note shall not exceed the limit prescribed by the committee on the face of the note. Article 4: The due date of the public note shall not be later than the thirtieth day after the date of issuance. Article 5: The committee is the payer of the public note and is responsible for payment in accordance with the wording on the public note. Article 6: The public note payment fund shall be prepared by the committee. Article 7: After the committee pays the public note, it may immediately recover the same amount from the original issuing bank and issue a new public note at the same time. Article 8: The provisions of Section 2 of Chapter 2 of the Bills of Exchange Law regarding the endorsement of bills of exchange shall apply mutatis mutandis to public notes, except for Article 32. Article 9: If the holder of a public note loses the public note due to fire, theft, loss in transit, or other accidents, he may prepare a petition stating the reasons to the committee and request suspension of payment. The foregoing provisions shall not apply to public notes that have been paid or accepted by the committee. Article 10: If the public note is lost and payment is suspended, the person who lost the note shall publish it in two or more famous newspapers agreed by the association for a period of three days, declaring it invalid. At the same time, a reputable guarantor shall be invited to provide a written guarantee. After three months, if there is no dispute, the committee may be requested to pay the money. Article 11: Member banks may use the public notes they receive as collateral to obtain full loans from the committee. Article 12: The public note that has not yet expired may be discounted by the public note holder to the committee. Article 13: The public note discount rate shall be determined and announced by the committee on a daily basis. Article 14: These regulations shall be implemented with the same effect when they are resolved and revised by the representatives of the member banks (New Voice News Agency Note: These regulations were revised on May 25 of this year). Annotation: According to the provisions of Article 32 of Section 2 of Chapter 2 of the Bills of Exchange Law, it is only used for bills of exchange. Its provisions are as follows: [The endorser may record one person in the place of payment as a preparatory payment].

Attached Public Note Style (New Voice News Agency Photo)

Opening of the Cooperative Enterprise Experimental Zone 152

The ceremony was held yesterday at the Second Civilian Residence

The cooperative enterprise experimental zone sponsored by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau held an opening ceremony at the Second Civilian Residence on the west end of Luban Road. Zhu Yuting of the Land Bureau, Zhang Yichen of the Rite Teaching Association, Shen Ruoxu and Xiao Zhiqing of the Municipal Farmers' Association, Wu Bochao of the Sixth District Tea Workers' Union, residents Xu Huanwen and Yao Fuwen, cooperative members Chen Busheng, Lv Xin, and Lv Shunjie, Wu Huanru, Zhang Binghui, Wang Gang, Zhang Zhenyuan, Chen Zeyi, and other staff members of the Social Affairs Bureau, as well as more than 300 guests from all walks of life, including Lu Huaiqi, Xu Ziqing, Du Jimei, and Zhang Qiuyu, were present. After the report by Chairman Zhang Binghui, Xin Juexian reported on the establishment of the Second Civilian Residence Cooperative. The Second Civilian Residence in Shanghai was completed in January 1931. All the residents are coolies and laborers. The Director Wang, in view of the difficult living conditions of the residents and the exploitation of the middlemen, proposed on March 3 of the same year to organize the Shanghai Civilian Consumer Cooperative to improve the living conditions of the residents, and it was approved by the Social Affairs Bureau. Subsequently, on March 13, the preparatory office of the cooperative was established, and preparatory personnel were appointed to actively prepare. However, due to the difficult living conditions of the residents, they were unable to join the cooperative. Although Director Wang and the preparatory personnel worked hard to promote it, few people joined. As a result, only 20 people, including Cui Zhaoding, were recruited as basic members. On May 14 of that year, an inaugural meeting was held, and Wang Gengchang and others were elected as directors. They immediately started to work, but the capital was only more than 500 yuan. After purchasing the necessary equipment for the cooperative, there was only more than 300 yuan of working capital left, so the scope of the business, although expanding, was to first set up an oil, sauce, cigarette, paper, and groceries department, which was announced to open on June 1. At the same time, they continued to solicit members in order to gradually expand the business and develop the cooperative. However, things did not go as planned, and nothing was achieved. The business was also very bleak. At that time, it was almost impossible to support it. Later, the board of directors used the method of increasing income and reducing expenditure. In addition to tightening expenses, the firewood, charcoal, barber, and food departments were entrusted to members to operate separately, and a surplus was taken from each month. Thus, the cooperative was able to survive the difficulties. Since then, through the prudent management of the board of directors, a hot water department was added in early January 1932, and the business began to progress. However, not long after, the January 28th Incident occurred, and the residents moved away one after another. On February 4, the cooperative and all departments announced their closure. Later, in April, it was heard that the ceasefire agreement had been concluded, and the cooperative reopened. However, at this time, about 100 households of residents had moved out of the residence due to the war, and the number of consumers suddenly decreased. The business of the cooperative was greatly affected. Although one employee was taken away to try to reduce expenses, it was still difficult to maintain. Some members and directors were also scattered due to the war, which made the strength of the cooperative even weaker. At the same time, the firewood and charcoal and barber departments also closed one after another due to the bleak business. The hot water department also suffered a large loss due to lack of management experience. At this time, the cooperative was like a candle in the wind, surrounded by danger. Later, through the painstaking planning of the directors in office, the hot water department was entrusted to members in May, and the surplus paid by the department each month barely covered the expenses. Thus, the cooperative was able to escape the danger. Not long after, although the food department closed down due to the bleak business, it did not have much impact because the residents gradually moved in and the consumption increased. By November, the business gradually improved, and each month's income, after deducting expenses, still had a slight surplus. However, at this time, the Finance Bureau's reorganization of the rent problem involved the cooperative's hot water department's rental housing. Later, with the maintenance and mediation of the competent authorities, it was able to pass safely. In April of this year, it was ordered to subordinate the cooperative to the cooperative enterprise experimental zone in this city. The name of the cooperative was changed to the Second Civilian Residence Cooperative of the Shanghai Cooperative Enterprise Experimental Zone. On June 3, a members' meeting was convened to discuss the reorganization issue. After the resolution, it was decided to actively reorganize the society. Subsequently, 19 members, including Wang Zhenchang, were recruited, and the first members' meeting after the reorganization was held on June 15. Yi Juexian and others were elected as directors, and it was resolved to take over the old society on June 30 and open the new society on July 3. In terms of business, the credit and consumption departments are currently being operated first. The credit department handles social credit loans, and the consumption department, in addition to the original business, plans to expand the food, firewood, charcoal, barber, food, hot water and other businesses. After a discussion by the board of directors, it was considered that the barber, food, hot water and other businesses lacked management experience and were difficult to operate. Therefore, it was decided to entrust the three businesses of barber, etc., to members to operate separately. All the business surplus of each business unit is reported to the cooperative by the operating members at the end of the month. Thanks to the efforts of the operating members, the three barber, hot water, and food services were able to open on schedule. As for the three items of food, firewood, charcoal, and credit loans, because the cooperative has only raised more than 300 yuan of share capital at present, it is not enough to maintain the original business, and the expansion of the business is still pending. However, the solicitation of the society should continue to be made in order to increase the society's capital and promote the society's affairs. Subsequently, the board of directors resolved to apply to the Social Affairs Bureau for a loan of 800 yuan in accordance with the city's cooperative enterprise experimental plan, using 500 yuan as capital for expanding the food and firewood and charcoal businesses, and 300 yuan as a credit loan fund. As soon as the funds are in place, they will be held immediately. Looking at the situation of the cooperative in the past two years, I don’t know how many difficulties it has gone through. Fortunately, with the efforts and struggles of all the members and the vigorous maintenance of the competent authorities, it has been able to survive to this day. In the future, in addition to hoping that all members will continue to work hard and the competent authorities will do their best to instruct them, I also hope that all sectors will give me guidance from time to time, so that the business of the cooperative can develop day by day, and the cooperative business of this city can also gradually progress. Next, more than ten people, including Zhang Yi, Shen Ruolu, etc., gave speeches, which were slightly longer.

Bulletin of the Central Cholera Prevention Institute 153

First Time

The first bulletin of the Central Cholera Prevention Institute said: (1) Although no true cholera has been found in Shanghai this year, all parties have been asking the institute whether the epidemic has occurred and the prevention procedures of the health agencies. This bulletin briefly describes all the preparations and conditions that have been taken. (2) Liu Ruiheng, Director of the Department of Health, convened a meeting of all health leaders at the First Hospital of the Red Cross Society on Haige Road a few days ago. In addition to Li Tingan, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, Mr. Mildon, Director of the Health Department of the Public Concession Engineering Bureau, Lapo, Director of the Health Department of the French Concession Engineering Bureau, Wu Liande, Director of the Seaport Quarantine Administration, and Yan Fuqing, President of the First Hospital of the Red Cross Society, Mr. Pauls, Representative of the Health Department of the League of Nations in China, also attended. It was resolved to organize two committees, one for immunological research, specializing in exploring the source of infectious diseases, and one for propaganda, specializing in promoting the development of public health education for the people. (3) The two committees have each held two meetings by June 30. The Propaganda Committee resolved that the three health agencies should print more leaflets and advertisements, and publish more articles in Chinese and Western newspapers to attract public attention. In addition, they will borrow radio stations to broadcast speeches by health officials and borrow public places where tourists gather, such as playgrounds and roof gardens, to show cholera films so that everyone can get common sense about cholera prevention and control. (4) The Immunological Research Committee resolved that experts from various health agencies should study various disease problems, such as water analysis, human bacteria mail, stool examination of healthy people and patients with watery diarrhea, clinical diagnosis research, meteorological research, and research. The water inspection team worked at the Lister Institute of Preventive Medicine. According to its report, from April to June 25, a total of 85 water samples from the Huangpu, Yangshupu, Xujiahui, Hongkou, and Zhabei rivers were tested, all using bacteriological methods. Although water vibrios were also found in the water, they were different from cholera vibrios after cultivation. This type of water vibrio was also found in the ponds and creeks in Zhabei. This study is still being actively conducted to clarify the relationship with cholera vibrios and its future development. (5) The cholera bacteria mail team has examined hundreds of stools of healthy people, but no cholera vibrios or cholera-like vibrios have been found. Recently, special attention has been paid to the analysis of the stools of patients with watery diarrhea. (6) According to the meteorological research team, in the 47 years of cholera epidemics in Shanghai (from 1886 to 1932), there was a major cholera epidemic every four years, which can be seen in 1887, 1890, 1902, 1914, 1923, 1926, 1929, and 1932. The years 1893, 1909, 1919, and 1925 were slightly different. In the past seven years, high temperatures have favored cholera epidemics, and low temperatures have eliminated cholera, but it cannot be generalized. When there is little rainfall in spring and winter, there will be a major cholera epidemic, and when rainfall increases, less cholera will be found. According to calculations, there was a lot of spring rain in 1933 (this year), so the cholera epidemic should not be severe. (7) Shanghai will have a total of seven cholera hospitals open in early July, with 1,000 beds. We sincerely hope that this year's work will not be as tense as last year. (8) The Shanghai Waterworks Company has agreed to supply drinking water to the poor in the east and west districts to prevent the spread of cholera. The French Concession also has free tap water facilities as last year to supply drinking water. The Shanghai Zhabei Water and Electricity Company also tried to supply drinking water to the poor at the lowest cost to seek popularity. (9) The Public Concession Health Department stated that from July 1, all patients with watery diarrhea must be reported. The Shanghai Municipal Health Laboratory has tested 56 stools of patients with watery diarrhea, but no cholera vibrios have been found so far. (10) Cholera vaccination is very active. Vaccination is free. As of May 31, the number of vaccinations is listed on the left: Shanghai City 93,962, Public Concession 66,723, French Concession 24,626, totaling 185,311. (11) Shanghai has a total of 47 suspected cholera patients, Hankou has two, but after bacterial examination, they are not true cholera. Shantou also reported two cases, Hangzhou four cases, and Yantai one case, but none of them have been examined by bacteria. (12) The Central Cholera Prevention Institute used to issue a bulletin once a week. Now, since there is no cholera outbreak, it is temporarily set to issue a bulletin once a month. The second cholera bulletin will be released in one month. If cholera is found, it will still be changed to a weekly report.

Chamber of Commerce Fourth General Meeting Resolves to Use Chinese for Insurance Documents 159

Requesting Government to Order Compliance

Based on the resolutions of the Fourth General Meeting, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a petition to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Social Bureau yesterday, stating: Regarding the request: The Chamber held its Fourth Members' Representative Meeting on the 25th of this month. The Shoe Leather Nail and Last Trade Association (Yuan Hongjun), the Tree and Rattan Industry Association (Zhu Huainan), and others jointly proposed that insurance documents should uniformly abolish foreign languages and use Chinese. They requested that the relevant authorities promptly issue an order for strict implementation. The petition stated: Regarding the matter of insurance documents uniformly abolishing foreign languages, the Chamber has handled it on record many times. However, various insurance companies have ignored it and have not complied. They still provide policyholders with documents written in foreign languages as valid proof. After policyholders obtain these incomprehensible foreign documents, they are completely ignorant of the records and conditions within the policy. In the event of an accident, the insurer uses these one-sided words and misinterpreted texts to evade all responsibility and act as a shield for deducting claims. In recent years, disputes and arguments arising from insurance compensation issues have been frequently reported in newspapers. This is all because policyholders only rely on the persuasion of intermediaries when purchasing insurance and hold mysterious foreign insurance policies without understanding the details. Therefore, insurance documents are an important contract to be observed by both the policyholder and the insurance company. They are of great importance to the people's lives and property. It is only right that policyholders should fully understand the details in the documents. Furthermore, all insurance companies, whether Chinese or foreign, since they operate in China and absorb Chinese customers, and the policyholders are all Chinese, should use Chinese to respect our national identity and preserve our national essence. This is the appropriate course of action. Therefore, insurance documents and all attached regulations should uniformly abolish foreign languages and use Chinese. We request that the relevant authorities promptly issue an order for strict implementation. Based on the above reasons, we hereby jointly and formally propose that it be submitted to the General Meeting for resolution. After discussion, it was agreed that the reasons stated in the proposal are indeed valid. However, with the presence of numerous Chinese and foreign insurance companies at sea, completely abolishing foreign languages may not be practical. It is proposed to amend it to use both Chinese and foreign languages. In case of doubt, the Chinese version should prevail. We request that the competent authorities issue an order for implementation. This would be in the public interest.

丨The case is adjourned to the 14th for further hearing丨

Then, the victim Shen Mengyi filed a case, proving the previous situation, and identified defendants Mao Zipei, Gao Changsheng, and Chen Wang in court as those who guarded him. These people guarded him during the day with two people, and two more were added at night. The injured bandits being treated in the hospital were also guards. However, the appearance of Wu Decheng was very similar to Wu Guiling and Wu Qiling from his hometown, but he could not confirm whether he was one of the two. Judge Feng checked the confessions, questioned the defendants briefly, and ordered them to be remanded in custody for further investigation in fourteen days.

The Western police chief, at approximately 1:00 AM, led a team of Chinese and Western detectives to the address. However, Yang had already absconded with his family, thus evading capture. There was no one in the house. Only seven bags of poison, weighing four pounds, half a box of raw red powder, three bags of heroin, one large bag of yellow powder, five baking trays for pills, one baking box, one lead wire tray, two bamboo joints, one small scale, and thirteen white cloth bags were seized, along with one pill-making machine. All were taken to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Second Special District Court. After review by the judge, it was ordered that all the seized items be destroyed and that the police station issue an arrest warrant for the main suspect and severely punish him.

A Mr. Chen Apprehended 165

Specializing in the sale of red pills, Mr. Chen, knowing that it would be difficult to gain a foothold since the French Concession Police had strictly prohibited it, secretly dispatched his gang members to sell them secretly, and then went into hiding in private rooms. Immediately, more Chinese and Western detectives were dispatched to apprehend Chen and take him to the police station for detention pending investigation.
