Free Talk

Thoughts on Reading the National Periodical Catalog 275

— Another Realm

One day, there was an advertisement in the Shenbao for Modern Bookstore selling national periodicals. I counted the catalog, and there were a total of 200 kinds. In my opinion, this catalog is quite complete, and almost all of the more famous periodicals are in it.

When I usually go to Neishan Bookstore, I am often amazed by the abundance of Japanese periodicals. Reading this catalog now seems to give me great comfort. The New Culture Movement of the past 13 or 14 years has actually produced 200 kinds of periodicals. Who can say that the May Fourth Movement had no achievements?

Some people say that there is no freedom of speech in China, but are these 200 kinds of periodicals not a "clear proof" of freedom of speech?

There used to be a statistic that said that there were more than 240 kinds of periodicals published by Japan in the three northeastern provinces (China only had more than 40 kinds). This number is just the number of periodicals in the whole country now. Naturally, we don't need to feel ashamed of this. Imperialism has economically invaded us for 80 years, but we still have a few yarn and silk factories. Comparing this, we can feel calm and at peace.

I have not run a bookstore, so I don't know how the sales of these periodicals are. Chinese booksellers often keep this business a secret, and it is actually impossible to count. Fortunately, there is already a catalog of 200 kinds. Our ancient civilized country is already quite proud.

Of course, we cannot say that these are all cultures under the command knife, but one thing can be asserted, that is, the command knife is always waving in front of you. A fool who is unwilling to be protected will have your freedom canceled sooner or later.

Therefore, humor is the smartest method. You can find a lot of humor in here. This makes us feel infinite sympathy, but it also shows the suffering that the era has given to writers!

Holding this catalog, I couldn't help but feel lost for a long time.

A Difficult Problem (A Kyogen Parody) 276

— Da Wu

Characters: Teacher (Protagonist)

Students A, B, C, D.

Teacher: I am the teacher here. It is true that my two shoulders cannot carry burdens, and my hands cannot lift baskets. I rely on a thin mouth to make a living and eat. There are not many students in the school, but they are all cunning and strange. They usually don't take me seriously and only make trouble. It is really difficult to deal with them. I need to think of a good way to rectify this academic atmosphere. Let me think, let me think. I've got it, I've got it. Let me come up with some difficult problems and ask them to solve them. If they can solve them, then that's fine. If they can't, I'll take the opportunity to severely reprimand them to avenge the troubles they've caused me. Fortunately, now the graduation examination is in full swing. I'm not afraid that these young boys will not obey. This is really a good plan, a good plan. So how should I come up with the difficult problems? I've got it, I've got it. Let me call them out and test them. Ahem, ahem, are the students all here?

Students A, B, C, D: We're all here.

Teacher: Then, let's start the class.

Students: Then, let's start the class.

Teacher: So today's first lesson is drawing.

Students: Drawing? Great.

Teacher: The summer vacation is coming soon, so let's have a test today.

Tomorrow, we'll take the graduation examination, so we can be prepared.

Students: Then please give us the problem, teacher. Please make it as easy as possible.

Teacher: Of course. I'll draw a dog on the blackboard first. Okay, it's done.

Students: No, no, teacher, you drew it wrong, you drew it wrong. Tsk! Tsk!

Teacher: What's wrong? What's wrong?

Students: Teacher's dog is missing a tail. Rabbits don't have tails, but dogs have tails.

Teacher: Then, you fill it in. That's the problem. Each person is only allowed to fill it in once, and you all have to be blindfolded. Those who fill it in correctly will get 100 points.

Student A: Good, good. This test is so easy. Let me go first.

Teacher: Let you go first. Blindfold yourself. Okay, fill it in.

Student A: It's done.

Students B, C, D: Ha, no, no, he filled in the dog's tail on the dog's back. Get down, get down.

Student B: He didn't fill it in well. Let me do it now. I will definitely fill it in correctly.

Teacher: Let you do it. Blindfold yourself, fill it in.

Student B: Okay, it's filled in.

Students C, D: No, no, he put the dog's tail on the dog's head. What a joke, what a joke. Let us do it, let us do it.

Teacher: Blindfold yourself. Okay.

Student C: It's done.

Students A, B: No, no. He's even worse than us. He put the dog's tail in the dog's mouth. No, no.

Student D: Let me do it, let me do it. If you can't do such an easy thing, what's the matter? I will definitely be better than all of them. I will definitely be first.

Teacher: Wait a minute, blindfold yourself. Ahem, fill it in.

Student D: It's done. Is it right?

Students A, B, C: Tsk, tsk, he's even further off. His tail is simply separated from the dog's body. Idiot, idiot.

Student A: Then, I filled it in the closest. I should be first.

Student B: I should be second.

Student C: Although I put the tail in the dog's mouth, it's still on the dog's body. I'm third.

Student D: Although I put the tail on the dog's body, there is still a tail, but I'm stronger than the teacher. The teacher didn't even draw the tail.

Students A, B, C: Then, the teacher is too bad. Let's drive the teacher away, let's drive the teacher away.

Teacher: Hey, this is a difficult problem. I specially gave it to you to fill in.

Students: What difficult problem? It's clear that you didn't draw it well yourself, and you forgot to draw the tail. Drive him away, drive him away. Drive him away, drive him away!

Random Notes on Reading 277

— Xiao Xue

(I)

Before the January 28th Incident, the poet Wang Tongzhao had been to the Northeast. There, he met a military officer who was his classmate from more than ten years ago. When they talked about the inevitable outbreak of the war in the Northeast, his friend emphasized:

[China can fight. It needs China to abandon the ports on the coastline, lure the enemy to land warfare, and use the power of Chinese soldiers and civilians to avoid direct wars, conduct attacks and irregular struggles, which can definitely be done, but considerable sacrifices are inevitable. The government should move to Sichuan. Holding on to it in the Central Plains, if we can persevere for more than a year and a half, even without the intervention of other countries, Japan will have no strength.] (Spring in the North, page 108)

According to the author, this person is someone who [works hard to exert his strength and implements things step by step]. Compared with the method of moving the capital to Luoyang, his plan can be said to be more thorough and more practical. No matter how much strength the Japanese have, they will not be able to [take Chengdu] for at least a year and a half, which is a fact that everyone will believe. I don't know why this military officer did not offer this proposal to the authorities at that time, so that the non-resistance doctrine and the three-capital doctrine could not be the sole precedent.

(II)

The triangular love novelist Zhang Ziping recently published his essay [Old Woman in Jiangbei] in a certain newspaper, writing about the death of an old woman who washed clothes. He felt three changes in his emotions after hearing the news of the death of the old woman in Jiangbei.

First, he heard about the old woman's lifelong asceticism and her death from postpartum disease. He [couldn't help but feel very sympathetic] and complained a lot, taking up the cause of the poor.

Second, the tone of the writing changed, and he remembered that this old woman had [instigated their long-used eldest sister to leave] and [instigated the female servant they had then hired] to leave, so he felt that [that old woman was too hateful] and [not worthy of death,] and [almost all of his sympathy and sighing disappeared].

Third, the tone of the writing changed again, and he regretted his [base and cruel feelings], greatly rebuked himself, and said: [What cruel animals humans are,] and [forgave] her behavior that was unfavorable to him during her lifetime.

Some people advocate petty-bourgeois revolutionary literature. I think this article is the most typical, and it is also a new formula for the author's later works, which was produced following the formula of his early love novels. Therefore, I specially recorded it.

Creative Novel

Ordinary Things 278

— Dan Guo Sun

(I)

In a flat-roofed house, there were six or seven men and women, each supporting their bodies in different ways, sitting, standing, and lying on the opium couch, talking leisurely. What were they talking about? They were talking about the current news of the fighting in Zhabei, and to be more precise, they were talking about the legendary news of the fighting in Zhabei. The posture of one person talking was as if he was sketching how a horse unexpectedly won the champagne at the racetrack. The posture of another person talking was as if he was describing how a small boat miraculously escaped a hurricane outside the Wusong Estuary. As for the others, they seemed to be expressing that their ears were not empty, so they just waited for someone to talk and immediately added to it. Some seemed to be expressing that their concern for the current situation and for national affairs was not indifferent, so they showed various expressions while listening. However, the light of the electric light in the house could prove that the emotions of these people were not as tense and active as the sound of gunfire they were hearing!

Suddenly, the middle-aged man lying on the opium couch, after taking a puff of opium, stretched out his flat and hoarse voice, as if sighing and exhaling:

[The sound of cannons seems to have started earlier tonight... It's probably not even nine o'clock yet... The rumbling sound is especially frightening, maybe no one is walking on the street without a curfew...]

After he finished speaking, he sighed again, and the air in the house seemed to suddenly become quiet again. No one had the interest to utter a word. After a few seconds of silence, the middle-aged man changed his tone and asked:

[Do you know Shou Zichun, Bo Tang?]

[I know him, Dad.] A young man sitting next to the table quickly turned around and replied to him sincerely: Then he showed a puzzled expression and asked: [Is Dad talking about Shou Zichun who used to be a counselor in the Ministry of the Navy?]

[I don't know about that; but I know he is now working at... Kenye Bank as... something...]

[That's right, Dad; he's from Fujian, right?]

[That's right, a Fujianese. He asked me to have dinner with him in the next day or two... He mentioned you to me today.]

[I haven't seen him for two months... Did Dad just meet him recently?]

[It's been about two or three months... before the war... I met him several weeks ago. He's a good person, always with that smiling round face, red and interesting, and his body is also interestingly short...]

After he finished speaking, he aimed his opium pipe at the opium lamp to smoke the newly prepared opium. Bo Tang did not understand why his father, Yao Yongsun, would know Shou Zichun, because the paths of these two people were too far apart. However, because Yongsun's life had too many mysterious stories, Bo Tang did not feel any curiosity at this time to inquire carefully, so he turned back to chat with the other people. However, Yongsun smoked opium and burned opium while secretly reviewing how he and Zichun had met in the first place.

Yongsun was originally the son of a high-ranking official of two generations in the late Qing Dynasty. Needless to say, his youth was a life of a young master; when his adulthood arrived, the Qing Dynasty had just been overthrown. Since he could not enjoy the life of being born into privilege and wealth, he simply continued to live in Shanghai to taste the taste of debauchery. Therefore, his adult life was also like that of a young master. After mixing like this for more than ten years, he was already a man approaching fifty years old, but his life had not changed from beginning to end. He did not become a politician, let alone a bureaucrat, nor did he become an entrepreneur. He only changed fresh methods every year to enjoy the ever-changing debauchery in Shanghai, and constantly spent thousands and thousands of foreign money from his family on the Bund. Therefore, his middle-aged life was still like that of a young master. Presumably, those men and women in Shanghai who parasitized in public places, as long as they saw the black car with the two license plates numbered one hundred and eleven approaching their door, everyone knew that it was the arrival of Yao Third Young Master - the name "Yao Third Young Master" had not changed for more than thirty years in various public places in Shanghai! On a certain winter night in 1930, this double-numbered 111 black car took Yongsun into the gate of 281 Foch Road. Once Yongsun entered this magical place, which should occupy a section of the [Shanghai Little History], he was habitually led to the hall on the south side of the upstairs. Immediately, two waiters in white shirts and black pants ran up to him to take his hat and coat. Subsequently, he raised his head, which consisted of three things: the eyebrows of a beautiful woman, the nose of a Jew, and the forehead of a god of longevity, and leisurely walked to the long table surrounded by many men and women. From the seats that the men and women had left empty for him, he grabbed one at random and sat down.

Comments

Youthful Desires 279

— Jian Yin

Desire is something everyone possesses. Because of desire, people disregard their possessions and lives, employing all possible means to attain it, striving to realize the object of their desire immediately. However, humans are insatiable creatures, so desire is limitless. Therefore, human struggles gradually become unavoidable. The more desires one has, the fiercer the competition. This is a very obvious direct proportion, especially for young people in general. They have the springtime of their lives; they need a beautiful environment and a comfortable life, so they also plunge into the crowd to pursue their desires.

Desire is certainly needed by everyone, but excessive enjoyment and undue demands are undoubtedly harmful to people's futures.

Young people are the pillars of the country's future and the pride of today's society. However, placed in this dazzling and complex environment, on the journey of pursuing their desires, if they stray onto a despicable path, it will bury a lifetime of happiness. How terrible is that! Therefore, regarding all desires, we must recognize which are proper and which are improper. Now, let us discuss them separately as follows:

Regarding proper desires, they can be roughly divided into two types:

(1) The evolution of intellectual society follows the wheels of culture. We rely solely on the limited knowledge gained from school to keep up with the rapidly advancing culture, which is clearly like sighing at the vast ocean. Therefore, in addition to the rigid knowledge of school, we must closely examine and experiment with society in practice to make up for the deficiency of our own intellectual famine. Therefore, enlightened young people also feel that to avoid being left behind by society, the only way is to constantly seek knowledge. We believe that this phenomenon, this desire for knowledge, is very admirable.

(2) After vocational youth leave the school of happiness, the first thing they feel is most needed and most urgent is the issue of occupation. However, in this era of declining production and societal upheaval, finding a suitable position is very difficult. But on the other hand, the lack of talent is felt everywhere, and finding talent is truly not easy. The creation of this contradictory phenomenon is actually due to the fact that those seeking employment fundamentally lack genuine basic knowledge. Naturally, in modern society, apart from a few who have the connections to stand on a group of planting party and private interests, the necessary condition is still that young people themselves must first have genuine knowledge. Therefore, if we want to seek a noble profession, we must first possess genuine knowledge. The meaning of life's happiness is the reward of hard work. Therefore, occupation is needed by everyone and is also a desire that young people should have.

Regarding improper desires, there are three types:

(1) Marriage Marriage is considered by young people to be the most important and sweetest thing in life, so they do not hesitate to abandon their studies in order to find their individual partner. Although marriage is an important matter, I believe it can only damage the will of young people. I am not opposed to marriage, but it is not suitable for young people. I believe that young students who are studying should focus on their studies. Otherwise, they will lose sight of one thing while attending to another, and the result will only be increased trouble. Therefore, our conclusion is that marriage is important to young people, but it should be avoided during the study period, so I cannot consider it proper.

(2) Vanity The word "vanity" does not know how many young people it has harmed. Because they are influenced by vanity, they throw proper learning to the back of their minds, follow the trend, and everyone only cares about external beauty, sacrificing a lot of money and time, but without any hesitation. In addition to seeking external beauty, they are no longer willing to ask or hear about other things. Those who seek knowledge are merely doing so in name only, and they are satisfied when they get a diploma. This morbid state will cause several tragedies for young people and bury many crises in society. It is the leader of sin for both oneself and others. Therefore, vanity is an improper desire, and we should eradicate these ideas.

(3) Extravagance People's concept of loving beauty is born of nature. Therefore, people's love of beauty and cleanliness is also inevitable. However, excessive pursuit of beauty leads to the path of extravagance, which is also a common disease of modern youth. Because they are accustomed to extravagance, they regard money as dirt, spending hundreds of dollars at a time, as if it were mud and sand. This poison, if minor, harms the individual's family, even to the point of bankruptcy and ruin. If major, it poisons society, the country, and even leads to the decline of the country's lifeline. Therefore, a luxurious life can make young people's will depressed, and the desire for extravagance can lead to the degradation of young people's personality.

If they are unrestrained and indulge in wine, sex, and lust all day long, they will inevitably injure their bodies without realizing it. As a result, they will become exhausted, their spirits withered, and their brains depleted, abandoning their studies, and eventually they will be unable to recover, regretting it for life. This kind of young person is originally

Seeking their own death, which need not be said by me.

Receipt 280

— Yi

Dense dark clouds covered everything on earth. Lightning flashed constantly, and thunder rumbled. People cooling off in front of the steps, afraid of the downpour, rushed like bees into the dark and lightless Japanese house. The heat of the street, washed by the rain god, was all driven into the houses. The heat inside the house increased sharply, causing annoyance, like ants on a hot pot, unable to sit or stand still. The dark clouds slowly crept eastward, and the lightning and thunder also stopped. The rain also stopped. The twinkling evening stars all appeared in the sky.

People cooling off still enjoyed the gentle cool breeze, gesticulating and talking! They didn't feel the sting of poisonous mosquitoes as if they had lost consciousness!

Modern Celebrities' Paintings and Calligraphy II (in order of receipt of manuscripts)

Mr. Min Lengchan's Painting (Brief Biography) 281

Mr. Min Lengchan is sixty years old this year. He was young and traveled with many predecessors, and when he grew up, he studied a wide range of books, especially indulging in the study of Song Confucianism. After the age of fifty, he devoted himself to painting and calligraphy. In calligraphy, he followed the style of Yan and Su and later studied Zhang Cao. His painting does not adhere to any one school, but freely expresses his own thoughts. His brushwork uses the suspended arm and central tip, so both his calligraphy and painting are extremely vigorous and profound. Usually, when he paints for guests, he is very oblivious to the presence of others. He once discussed painting with me, saying that there is no other method for writing characters than drawing vertical and horizontal lines. Painting is also like this, so those who can write characters can also paint. His high-mindedness is often like this.

It's getting deeper! All sounds were silent, except for the faint sound of distant dogs barking. A deathly silence was heard! Moonlight shone through the glass window, bathing the small room and stripping away the light of the bean lamp. Tossing and turning in bed made it impossible to fall asleep. I thought of reading a tasteless book, which had the magic power to induce sleep like a lullaby. Before I even started reading, I found a piece of paper that caused sorrow!

This is a receipt! This is the receipt from the last semester of my education five or six years ago! This is the last receipt of my life for schooling! Although the amount on the receipt is only fifty or sixty yuan, which is not enough for a pair of silk stockings or a bottle of perfume in the eyes of the rich, this receipt caused my parents to work hard, worry, and beg for pity before they raised enough money on the day before school started, received this receipt, and completed the last semester of my education. Unfortunately, at the age of eighteen or nineteen, my poor parents no longer worked hard, worried, begged, or pleaded for me. They have exhausted all their efforts and are now resting under the nine springs! It's too late to regret it! Poor students! Strive for your knowledge! Be thrifty with your expenses! Repay your old fathers and mothers for their hard work, worries, begging, and pleading, and serve society and the country!

Secret Poem 282

— Liang Yi

X School is a very famous middle school in Shanghai, with about a thousand students. Because there are so many students, the school rules are inevitably somewhat lax and cannot be strictly followed. As a result, ambiguous love affairs are often heard of, swallowing copper coins! Exchanging letters and making secret rendezvous! Hanging oneself! Also emerge endlessly. The school authorities, in view of this, specially organized a letter inspection committee. All letters must be reviewed by their | inspection committee staff | before they are returned to the students. Therefore, the general friends of lovers | dare to boldly use bribery in broad daylight. Watermelon seeds, peanuts, and other things to be sucked and chewed have all become their target objects. K is a very famous pretty boy in X Middle School, so of course his love affairs should be more than others, especially the love letters he exchanges can be second to none, worthy of being called unique. Therefore, the staff of the inspection committee also paid special attention to his letters, partly because he refused to bribe. But don't say there wasn't a single love letter, even family letters were rare to come by!

Saturday afternoon, as usual, is the school's Holiday. Everyone can see that his hair is extra shiny, his suit is also extra clean and straight, and his leather shoes are polished to a strange shine.

Their faces are covered with a layer of snow cream that looks like lime; this is to prepare to go to the park with their Love! Watch movies! Open a hotel… K certainly cannot be an exception, and his grooming skills are better than others, and his flattering surgery is also better than others, so today he is dressed as a handsome young man, in a suit and leather shoes, truly a fine young master of the world.

After the sound of a bicycle bell rang, the tea room's Ah San, holding a large bundle of letters, went to the inspection committee room like an arrow.

The scorching sun shrouded the playground. The entrance of the inspection committee room was crowded with people, as if they were facing a great disaster.

"Is there a letter for me?"

"Zhang, if there is a letter for me, please bring it to the dormitory for me."

The inspectors each looked spiritedly. The letters flew past like snowflakes one by one. Suddenly, a pink envelope was exposed in front of everyone's eyes, so everyone stared intently like they were dead. Ah! Inside, it turned out to be a very plain five-character律诗 poem. The original text reads:

What day is today,

How many days and nights are there?

Three days without seeing you,

I miss you all the time.

On the left side of the Falun Temple,

A scholar builds a garden residence.

Public affairs are not asked about,

The garden is accompanied by poetry and books.

Waiting to welcome hermits,

Do not delay your journey.

"Ah! If you read from the beginning, isn't it a love appointment letter saying, 'See you at the French Park at three o'clock today'!" The naughty C-kun shouted loudly as if he had suddenly realized something.

The truth of the case was immediately revealed, and everyone discussed it with啧啧 noises.

A burst of noisy bickering rose from the ground in K-kun's dormitory.

[Haha! What a cunning lover.]

[Hollow! Your skill is really not small. You can actually find such a lover.]

[Your Love is so silly]

K-kun slipped away with a red face and red ears!

When I stepped out of the dormitory, a faint noise was still spinning in the entire corridor.

A' Gou 283

—

The idiot A' Gou hanged himself. In this day and age, the hanging of one or two people like A' Gou is not a sensational event, especially since he was a criminal?

A' Gou drifted from Shandong to Shanghai, selling his labor and exchanging it for a few pancakes every day. He worked all day long, and time passed so quickly. A' Gou's youth was buried in the ruthless wind and snow. Although he had iron muscles and a strong mind, he gradually felt tired.

In his forties, the idiot was squeezed out of the labor-selling workshop, and the sorrow of unemployment immediately weighed on him. It was already winter, and A' Gou hadn't had any pancakes today. He was only wearing a jacket, shivering and standing by the roadside, like a sick dog about to starve to death.

[As long as you are human, you should have clothes to wear and food to eat. Although the idiot is old, he can still work! Why starve to death?] As he passed by a restaurant, this silly idea attacked his silly brain. The nose smelled the fragrance of fish and meat. Fragrant, idiot, don't you want it? His already hungry eyes widened so much, and he stretched out his dirty hands and broke into the kitchen of the restaurant.

The idiot was sentenced to three months' imprisonment. He sat in a narrow and damp prison cell, stroking the iron bars that were only an inch in diameter. He smiled. [This is not bad. At least there is food to eat]. But the tattered old jacket became a problem. The idiot's old bones couldn't withstand such cold. Leave here, or I'll freeze to death if I stay any longer. The idiot's second thought. So he carried out sabotage work. Late at night, two bricks under the iron window were removed. With unknown strength, a big hole was opened in half an hour. The idiot smiled and climbed out, but the sharp north wind outside ruthlessly pounced on him again.

[Damn it, this wind, do you dare to block my way?] The idiot cursed angrily. As a result, the night guard heard him and caught him back, and he was beaten with a whip. The skin on his back was torn open, and iron chains were added.

[Why did you dig a hole in the wall and escape?]

[What? Escape. It's cold! I don't want to stay here.]

[This is the judgment of the law. You have to live here whether you want to or not.]

[I don't want to. I have to go out. You bully me for being an idiot, idiot!]

[You bastard!]

[Bastard? Why don't you come and stay for a few days? This is the idiot's confession in court.

That night, the idiot had a dream, dreaming that his dead father was waving to him. When he woke up, his legs were already frozen stiff. [Living like this is worse than dying. Dad wants me to go.] When the idiot thought of this, he untied his belt and tied it to the horizontal bar of the iron window, made a knot, and put it around his starved neck. The idiot smiled, and everything was resolved.

The idiot A' Gou hanged himself. In this day and age, the hanging of one or two people like A' Gou is not a sensational event, especially since he was a criminal?

Li Heizi, who used to live with A' Gou, told this story.

Under the Red and Green Lights (17) 284

— Xi Lin

(11) [Just listen to Mr. Chen's command for everything.]

Of course, early in the morning, Li Shiqiao and Wang Hua were [walking] on the road.

[Shiqiao, it's really a dead end. The pawnshops are all closed. Otherwise, if I took my wife's clothes, I could still pawn them for] two oceans. I only found eight coins by walking until twelve o'clock last night. Hu Yuanliang is considered generous. It's really not easy to borrow money now!] Shiqiao obviously had no interest in these words. He was thinking about a passionate speech to resist Japan and save the country. Wang Hua immediately changed his tone: [I heard that Lao Chen came from a worker background! What kind of person is he? What do you think of him?]

[I think he's okay. He still has some passion. He is firmly advocating resistance against Japan!]

[Passion?] Xue Wanghua knew what the so-called [passion] of politicians was. He really didn't need to explain to Shiqiao, so he smiled and stopped talking. They walked silently until they reached Chen's mansion.

They waited in the living room for more than half an hour before Chen Tianren strolled out step by step. The servant stood beside him and fanned the door curtain. This scene easily reminded people of the appearance of some high-ranking official appearing on the stage, with gongs and drums sounding loudly. Li Shiqiao and Wang Hua were indeed nervous. Chen Tianren's majesty has always been able to subdue young people, but it is also necessary to show friendliness in the midst of majesty. He let the young people sit down first, and then he sat opposite them, raising his neck and making a condescending posture.

[This is Comrade Wang Hua, the standing committee member and organization minister of the district,] the tall Li Shiqiao stood up first, and the short Wang Hua nodded five or six times to the opposite side. [Comrade Wang has been in Shanghai for many years and is very familiar with all sectors of society.]

Temporary silence.

In the past, yes, we felt the lack of unified leadership. So it is not easy to concentrate the quantity, so, so Comrade Li, we hope to unite the people of this city during this critical period of resistance against Japan, especially, especially the nationalists and the communists are using this opportunity to stir up trouble. Chen Tianren was getting quite bored listening, and knowingly gave a few noises of [Hmm] and turned his face to Li Shiqiao.
